'px' );</script><script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
function loadAdScripts() {
// ScriptWrapper
var s = document.createElement("script");
s.src = "https://scripts.scriptwrapper.com/tags/d1d871dc-893a-4819-8ef9-64fd69363a96.js";
s.async = true;
s.setAttribute("data-noptimize", "1");
s.setAttribute("data-cfasync", "false");
document.body.appendChild(s);
}
// Chỉ load khi scroll hoặc sau 3 giây
let loaded = false;
function triggerLoad() {
if (!loaded) {
loadAdScripts();
loaded = true;
}
}
window.addEventListener("scroll", triggerLoad, {once: true});
setTimeout(triggerLoad, 3000);
});
</script><script>
jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
$(document).on('copy', function(e){
var newText = "\nsavourthepho.com";
var clipboardData = e.originalEvent.clipboardData || window.clipboardData || e.clipboardData;
var originalText = window.getSelection().toString();
clipboardData.setData('text', originalText + newText);
e.preventDefault();
});
});
</script><span id="foxglobal"></span><script>
/* Cuộn mượt tới recipe */document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
const a = e.target.closest('.stp-jump');
if(!a) return;
const el = document.querySelector('#wprm-recipe-container, .wprm-recipe-container');
if(el){ e.preventDefault(); el.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth'}); }
});
/* Ẩn cụm quick nếu không có recipe block */document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
if(!document.querySelector('#wprm-recipe-container, .wprm-recipe-container')){
document.querySelectorAll('.stp-quick').forEach(el=>el.style.display='none');
}
});
/* Chèn rating “5 from X votes” ngay dưới H1 – bỏ hẳn “(… rating without comment)” */document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
if ( !document.body.classList.contains('single-post') ) return;
const title = document.querySelector('.entry-header .entry-title');
const src   = document.querySelector('.wprm-user-rating-summary'); // rating có sẵn phía dưới
if (!title || !src) return;
if (document.querySelector('.stp-rating-summary-top')) return; // tránh chèn lần 2
// Clone và dọn rác <style> + <svg width="0" height="0">
const clone = src.cloneNode(true);
clone.querySelectorAll('style').forEach(n => n.remove());
clone.querySelectorAll('svg[width="0"][height="0"]').forEach(n => n.remove());
// Ẩn/remove link “no comments” nếu có + gọt bỏ "( ... )" cuối chuỗi
const details = clone.querySelector('.wprm-user-rating-summary-details');
if (details) {
details.querySelectorAll('.wprm-user-rating-summary-details-no-comments').forEach(n => n.remove());
details.textContent = details.textContent.replace(/\s*\(.*\)\s*$/,'').trim(); // giữ lại “5 from X votes”
}
const wrap = document.createElement('div');
wrap.className = 'stp-rating-summary-top';
wrap.appendChild(clone);
title.insertAdjacentElement('afterend', wrap);
});
